It is classified as a woody - spicy composition.</p>

<p>Top notes: cinnamon and pepper wood. Heart: osmanthus, tobacco leaf, labdanum and incense. Base: vanilla, cedar, vetiver, patchouli, iso e super, cypriol and musk.</p>

It's got the signature PDM cinnamon note in the drydown that PDM is known for, also prominent in Althair and Oajan. To me, I actually get a major dried fruits feel from this, like dried oranges, dates or deep dark dried cherries. something of that nature.<br />
<br />
It's fruity, with an understated tobacco base that gives it a pretty masculine feel. It's a sweet smooth tobacco, the type that you have nostalgia about when you think of a cigar &amp; bourbon bar. It's a subtle frag as well, not beast mode performance, which is not a bad thing. This is much more suitable for everyday wear and office wear, unlike other tobacco frags. <br />
<br />
I feel this is closer to Spicebomb Extreme than Tobacco Vanille. In my opinion this smells nothing at all like tobacco vanille. <br />
<br />
This is a solid 7! I think it's good, but the internet really overhypes this brand.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2323771"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2323771#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2323655" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I’ve tried Spicebomb Extreme and Tom Ford’s Tobacco Vanille, I found them to be a little overbearing. Herod is definitely more subdued and inoffensive. This may be what affects the performance since this is definitely softer than most other fragrances that share this scent profile. <br />
<br />
Seems like a double edged sword in this matter, and I can see why people would choose other fragrances within this category such as the ones I mentioned over this because they perform better and have a more robust presence to them. I just prefer the elegance and intimacy of this one. I would still consider this way overpriced for what it offers though.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2322953"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2322953#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2321462" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0; border: none; margin: 0;"><!-- 71161633/perfume_incontent_6/perfume_incontent_6 --><div data-fuse="22384457079"></div></div><div id="parent2319358" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319358" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Pyroo"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1766375"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1766375.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Pyroo" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319358ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319358" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.81); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1766375">Pyroo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-17">10/17/24 21:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Somebody below said this is non original, buy Ambre Tabac instead. It's hilarious how some people quickly jump into the PdM hate without doing a bit of research. First of all, PdM does clone a lot of fragrance and I'm not defending PdM at all. But, you have to know that this particular one, Herod, was created in 2012 by master perfumer Olivier Pescheux. Meanwhile, Ambre Tabac was created in 2014 by Daniel Josier. So who's cloning who? If you know Olivier Pescheux, he is famous for being original and creative, so that's reason number two why that comment is just such a misinformation. Herod inspired a lot of similar fragrances but that does not mean that Herod is not original. Do some research before you shit talk or you'll look like a stupid clown.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2319358"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2319358#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318619" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2312752" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ALakota"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1565541.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ALakota" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Precious-Liquid/Salt-Pepper-80626.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.80626.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Salt & Pepper"title="Salt & Pepper"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2312752ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2312752" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1565541">ALakota</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-11">10/11/24 18:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Herod is interesting. I feel like the performance is not incredible, but not terrible, and I used to not like it, even though I blind bought several bottles at a good deal lol. It does have a strange thing going on that I can completely understand that some people will not dig. I have been sampling a ton of things in the mean time, and I came back to this stuff and I actually really love it now. To me the most detectable note I would say hits me as honey. I know it's not in the notes, but something about the vanilla and the other components hits me as a sort of raw honey accord. What I didn't like originally I guess was just its particular brand of "darkness" which I'm sure is related to the tobacco, though it still doesn't strike me as obviously tobacco, like some people are talking about ash trays and whatever. I don't get that at all. If I had to guess, it seems more like a dried smoking tobacco to me. Not leaf and not burnt or ashy. It just smells a bit daring in a good way, but probably to the right person specifically. Like I said, I used to not be crazy about it, but now I honestly love it, but respect that it will be polarizing because I've been there. Either way, it is certainly high quality, unique, artistic, and not too off the beaten path for those around you to be offended or question it very much. And the performance isn't too bad, honestly. It's in a good place and it lasts a while. People forget that some scent profiles simply can not be made too beastly, or you are going to alter the scent itself. PDM hit the mark with what they are trying to do here. Not a blind buy for most people, but to the right person this might be a grail. Anyone who is a fan of PDM and their style of doing things needs to at least sample it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2312752"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2312752#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2311618" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2254921" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="oliveeyes94"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2057320"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="oliveeyes94" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2254921ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2254921" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2057320">oliveeyes94</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-20">08/20/24 02:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So I was racking and reracking my brain about what juice reminded me of for a solid 3 or 4 wears on different occasions. Soon after the rather harsh opening spray it just felt so so familiar.<br />
<br />
Then it hit me!<br />
<br />
Who has tried the Double Platinum Cherry flavoured blunt wraps? Well, this smells exactly like those to my nose. There is obviously the tobacco, but its not burning, it's more dank with a certain damp quality.<br />
<br />
Unsure what exactly is giving the cherry accord, perhaps the cinnamon combined with the floral notes, but it's certainly there.<br />
<br />
The Iso-e super, which arrives a little later (especially when giving the sprayed area a little rub) is potent, and distracts from the initial cherry blunt wrap vibes.<br />
<br />
This is strong on my skin too - easily noticeable sillage for the first couple of hours, slowly making its way to a skin scent, at which point I scrubbed it. Even from the opening I wasn't a massive fan, but was curious about how that nostalgic scent was going to develop.<br />
<br />
I made the comparison elsewhere with Volutes by Diptyque, which is lighter and more airy. Much weaker too, becoming a skin scent within an hour on me.<br />
<br />
I just don't think I'm a big fan of this cherry, tobacco, shisha pipe accord which both of these fragrances have. Can imagine many people enjoying this if these notes are your jam. For something vaguely similar, but much classier and with better performance, I do love Chergui.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2254921"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2254921#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254468" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2217298">apalmaa</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-10">08/10/24 05:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Herod is a winter beast. Out of the more popular/well known niche brands, PDM’s big hitters (Layton, Carlisle, etc) are very well crafted, yet Herod is under appreciated while IMO it being the best out of the bunch. The tobacco is not that of a polarizing fragrance, but rather of a sweet, smooth cigar that sat in the humidor for just the right amount of time. It works perfectly in concert with the sweet-leaning spiciness of the cinnamon alongside the classic vanilla. While the opening is beautiful, I think this fragrance truly shines in the base. The vanilla and woody notes become more pronounced as the tobacco fades into the background. Overall, beautifully crafted fragrance. Amazingly smooth. 10/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2244763"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2244763#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2243426" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1748293">faris_fauzee</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-08">08/08/24 23:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>smell good, really good actually especially in the dry down, it is dark but not as dark as Amouage Royal Tobacco, the cinnamon note played a major role, this set it apart from Tom Ford Tobacco Vanille, the osmantus note gave it slight fruitiness (cherry like maybe?) and overall creaminess alongside that musk and slightly sweet boozy vanilla note. The dry down is where this get really good, that cypriol oil, vetiver and cedar wood gave it woodiness, slight earthiness and smokey facid together with all the other  notes involved.<br />
<br />
Is the tobacco note loud and present? The tobacco note is not that prominent to me, it is present but blended with all the note. I would go as far by saying that TF Tobacco Vanille is more tobacco than this. While some say this give off cigar like vibe, to me, if you wanna give off cigar vibe, Amouage Opus Royal Tobacco is the way to go. That is the closest you will get to a cigar like smell.<br />
<br />
It last on my skin yet sadly enough it doesn’t project well nor leaving a good trail of scent. To be honest, at first, I regretted buying this, even considering of reselling it. It cost a good amount of money even getting it through a discounter seller. But as time goes, maybe maceration happened and the performance gets better. Now Im happy having this is my collection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2243426"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2243426#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2242974" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1296418">EnsureESydney</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-12">07/12/24 23:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A key piece in my current wardrobe but I have to be honest and say my bottle is 5-6 years old.  I've been living off a 10mL discovery sample as well, of not too-lesser vintage, and so please don't take this as the way it necessarily is.  A tiny sample came my way recently (official PDM sample) and it wasn't the same as the juice I wear (although not bad from little I smelt; I simply lost patience with longevity on back of hand, to understand it more, and binned it after a couple of tries, content with what I already own).<br />
<br />
One of the first 'must have' frags I bought in this resurrected passion of mine in recent years.  Well stored since.  It was mind-blowing, then wonderful, then too weak, then too cherry as I drifted towards TF Tobacco Vanille samples and other things; then, after some time away, I wore, it gelled, and now I have peace of mind to enjoy it as an integral part of my Autumn/Winter wardrobe.  Unassailable until this juice runs out and my search for a replacement begins.<br />
<br />
If I was on a skiing holiday then I'd take my Amouge's for the day (sunny and dark) and this would be the piece that I'd wear, all tired, battered and bruised, by fireside in the evening, sipping on painkiller (lousy skier!).  A modern classic of tobacco, vanilla and cinnamon that is seductive, soothing and calming.  A king of intimacy.  Safely masculine but the door is open surely for women to enjoy.  Longevity is fine probably 6-7 hours on skin and more if sprayed heavily and on clothes.  A scent for the ages, and an Autumn essential for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2217134"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2217134#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2214951" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; However, Herod is more balanced in its lifespan and really alluring and sexy. Tom Ford upfront is much more vanilla and spice centric whereas this is more warm creamy tobacco.<br />
Herod can be worn throughout fall and winter months whereas Tobacco Vanille, is to me, exclusively December as it smells like Christmas in a bottle and for December there’s no other contender. <br />
<br />
Not much to say that hasn’t already been said. This is sexy, alluring, warm, sensual, mysterious, very well composed and executed. Performance can perhaps be better, but it’s not bad.<br />
<br />
Another exquisite release from PdM. 95% of their fragrances I’ve smelt are just very good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2207098"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2207098#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2206688" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1322412">Sajjad_Frag</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-03">07/03/24 02:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Overall Rating: 9.5/10<br />
<br />
Herod PDM is a sexy, delicious fragrance perfect for dates and dinner nights. Its rich and deep scent profile makes it ideal for the cooler months, though it may be a bit too intense for summer wear. Designed for both men and women, it leans more towards a masculine vibe. While it is somewhat expensive, the quality and experience it offers make it worth the investment.<br />
<br />
Ratings:<br />
- Longevity: Lasts 8-10 hours, earning a solid 9/10.<br />
- Projection: Projects to arm length for about an hour, rated at 6/10.<br />
- Scent: The scent is impeccable, deserving a 10/10.<br />
- Material Quality: Exceptional material quality, also rated at 10/10.<br />
<br />
Summary:<br />
Herod PDM stands out with its irresistible blend of sexiness and deliciousness, making it a top choice for intimate and special occasions. Its performance in longevity and quality is remarkable, although the projection could be stronger. With an overall rating of 9.5/10, this fragrance is a worthy addition to any collection for those who appreciate luxury and sophistication.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Tragic sillage and decent longevity, this would be better if it was way stronger</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2194100"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2194100#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2193233" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2193233" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="frankcoelho"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1712325"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1712325.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="frankcoelho" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Amouage/Interlude-Black-Iris-60929.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.60929.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Interlude Black Iris"title="Interlude Black Iris"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2193233ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2193233" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1712325">frankcoelho</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-19">06/19/24 12:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Herod has been a favorite of mine for quite some time. However, I unfortunately came across a recent batch that opened my eye toward something I've always ignored: BATCH VARIATION/REFORMULATIONS.<br />
<br />
It used to be a strong, long lasting fragrance. My current batch #3162540 and others I have compared it to (starting with digit #3 and 7 digits total) in other stores, have shown me that Herod DIED, which really is a shame. Several tests have given me 3-4h of very soft projection. I understand maceration and wearing does cause the fragrance to evolve and likely further develop the notes and performance, but not to the point where my bottle will be "moderate or even strong."<br />
<br />
Juice color is light, actually very light in color now. It used to be a nice ambary orange/brown. Rather oily, the new batch did not latch on my skin, but left this oily sheen. Clothes did not improve upon that performance (in contrast with how it affects other fragrances). I've sprayed a shirt of mine ~10x and, from that, 12h and a very light trail of the scent was observed.<br />
<br />
Again, I hope these few batches/bottles I have tried are not final and PDM recovers - or they'll have to come up with an Exclusif version of it. Very disappointed! My rating is still "OK" because of how lovely the beginning 30min-1h smell and the history behind what I used to experience with it. Other than that, total frustration.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2193233"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2193233#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2189801" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2189801" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="NunoRealinho"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1794811"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1794811.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="NunoRealinho" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2189801ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2189801" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1794811">NunoRealinho</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-16">06/16/24 04:44</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my first "review" of a perfume. After purchasing PDM Layton on the official website, I received a generous set of gifts (since it was my first order) and Herod stood out among all the others.<br />
<br />
I am by no means an expert in detecting notes, but the blend of all the ingredients is done fantastically. The cinnamon, tobacco, and vanilla present themselves in an addictive manner, and the perfume exudes class in every way. Reading many of the reviews here, I noticed that a lot of people complained about Herod's longevity and that it had been reformulated and wasn't worth the price. My sample had quite good performance (8 to 10 hours… or more), so I decided to take the risk. I bought Herod in October 2023 (Batch Code, for those interested, 3232540 from February 2023). And I couldn't be more satisfied with my purchase!<br />
<br />
I should also note that my skin has terrible chemistry for perfumes like Acqua Di Gio Profondo, Bleu de Chanel Eau de Parfum, or Intense Cedrat Boise (among others) where I can barely smell anything after two hours. In the case of Herod, although the projection is moderate, I can still smell it after 10 hours without any difficulty.<br />
<br />
I don't think any perfume is worth buying without trying it first (whether it's €20 or €200), not only because of the subjectivity inherent to our sense of smell but mainly because the chemistry of our skin is different. For any summery/fresh perfume, if I'm lucky, I can smell it for about 4 hours, but in this case, the longevity is excellent, and I think it was an excellent purchase despite it being an expensive perfume.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; The problem being, it is hitting all the right spots to me so I had bought a used bottled and found myself becoming intoxicated by it. I needed to smell it and use this fragrance.... so now I am buying backup bottles in fear of it not being there for my need. Obsession much?<br />
<br />
This is a Tobacco fragrance that has a creaminess to it laid on top of cinnamon-vanilla. It is a sweetened pipe tobacco that is a "wet" tobacco and is very appealing (at least to me). There are no notes of chocolate, but I get a cocoa powder vibe in this that is a bit gourmand like to me. It sits close to skin after a couple of hours. I wear this for myself and not to announce myself to others, though those close will definetely smell it. Do not be fooled, but you will still catch whiffs 6-7 hours later and still garner compliments.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2150050"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2150050#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2148039" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1723203">Psalzarulo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-07">04/07/24 16:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Another unique one from PdM. The first spray is harsh for a few seconds before morphing into a smoky gourmand that has a sweet top notes. It's one of those scents that confuses the palate at first but the airy cinnamon and rich, dark tobacco, incense, and labdanum create something that's cohesive and IMO pretty addictive. I really love PdMs ability to make such a strong set of notes and blending them with sweet, appealing notes to create something that is clearly masculine but also very sensitive and thought-provoking. <br />
<br />
Like a lot of Pam scents, it's strong enough to remind you it's there but not so strong that it's overpowering. it's also unique and bold enough to capture someones attention but as you get closer it's even more appealing and will pull you in.  It's bold and masculine but not obnoxious. I guess the moral of the story is that PdM is an expert in blending notes, even if they're not necessary pushing many boundaries. <br />
<br />
On dry down, the vanilla, cedar, and vetiver notes some out and it becomes a more dark, smoky scent. <br />
<br />
As with the other PdM scents I've sampled Herod is really nice but just missing something to make it truly great. I give it a 8.75/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2117531"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2117531#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2111754" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Captures only the most pleasant elements of tobacco and incense and blends them beautifully with vanilla and other spices.<br />
<br />
Herod just oozes maturity, class, and rugged masculinity. In my opinion it would be out of place on most men under 30 and many under 40. Test it first and be honest with yourself whether this suits your style and maturity level. IF you can pull it off, it's a 10/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2088307"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2088307#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2088278" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Its so smooth and nice, intoxicating to say the least. <br />
The tobacco is not ashy but rather extremely smooth along with the beautiful combo of vanilla and cinnamon.<br />
The scent is a 10 / 10 but there seems to be a problem with performance for some people, for example it lasted only a few hours on my dad's skin and had little to no projection while on my skin it did last around 8 hours with decent projection.<br />
I suggest that you try this one on your own skin and if it lasts a long time, go for it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2072480"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2072480#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2071584" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1817428">AllThatJaZZ</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-23">02/23/24 03:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>First of All Hail the legend Olivier Pescheux... his essence will live on immortalised in his creations. <br />
<br />
Herod opens with a rich projection of spicy cinnamon and moderate sweet accords. The incense accords slowly pops in bringing with it an airy floral note. Here the combination hangs around for the first hour or so and then finally the vanilla and tobacco accords kick in eventually resting in a woody spicy note with a slight vetiver accord which is where the similarities with frags like Spicebomb, Tobacco Vanille, Bvlgari MIB, Franck Boclet Tobacco are evident. <br />
<br />
The perfume has strong projection and is easy to wear. Smells great upclose and from a distance, works best in colder weather and lasts a long time that a decant is not really required. I go a max of 2 sprays on skin and get a great 8 to 10 hour Herod experience. Dope bottle design and fantastic sprayer. All in all an absolutely brilliant frag loved and complimented by many. <br />
<br />
A great alternative to the Herod DNA would be Divine Vanille from Essential Parfums. It's from the same perfumer, I would classify Divine Vanille as a lighter version of Herod which can be worn on warmer weather and it's a lot more affordable but Herod is still the KING🤘🤘</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1295740">RayCashhhh</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-13">02/13/24 06:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>When I first started off on my fragrance journey, I remember watching Demi Rawlings videos and she would constantly praise Herod as the best fragrance for men ever. While it turns out she was getting kickbacks for promoting it so much, the praise was entirely justified. Within a few months, the scent profile has become one of my favorites ever. Herod is a timeless classic for the colder months of the year. Could be worn by anyone 25 and up, in just about any occasion. The tobacco and vanilla combo paired with the other notes is so good there's not enough adjectives to describe it. As far as the scent itself, this is honestly an 11/10. <br />
<br />
Now here comes the bad part: the performance on the new batches is ABYSMAL. Gone in about an hour on my skin. At $350, the performance does not come close to justifying dropping that much bread on a new bottle. I haven't looked, but vintage batches probably cost an arm and a leg to obtain. I'm not doing any of that. Instead, there are some dupes out there that may not smell 100% as Herod, but perform much better at a fraction of the price. The Herod scent profile will forever remain a staple in my collection, just not Herod itself.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2060927"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2060927#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2059715" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The opening smelt like straight up cigarettes, and the drydown become more creamy and sweeter and became like those candles that smell good but still had that cigarette/tobacco note that tormented me. I initially wanted to blind buy this but do NOT and I repeat, do NOT buy this without smelling it first. To some it’s a masterpiece, and to others it’s disgusting. Choose your side carefully</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="2056131"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=2056131#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2055410" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1500063" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jaxxin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/342645"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.342645.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jaxxin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.16939.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Herod"title="Herod"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1500063ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1500063" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/342645">jaxxin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-02-08">02/08/22 07:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I have been sampling 20+ of the all time popular/highest rated men’s fragrances the last month or two. Creed, Tom Ford, Guerlain, Givenchy, Dior, Chanel, Malle, Dolce, Prada, etc etc <br />
<br />
Then last night I applied my sample of Herod. <br />
<br />
My eyes widened, jaw dropped. It smells so so so wonderful on me that it is viscerally stunning, almost dizzying. It is so much better than any of the other best of the best fragrances I’ve tried.<br />
<br />
Herod balances the best of the best dark Rich creamy elements but stays much less sweet than current trends (looking at you Tom Ford). It is dark but not heavy, smoky but not stale or acrid, sweet/fruity/floral but just a touch, edible but not cloying candy dessert, spicy and peppery but not sharp or offensive. <br />
<br />
Many say this is Tobacco plus Vanilla, but it is not and is much more. I would say it is centrally incense, which is tying together four or five different notes supported by two or three ingredients each. Much more indeed. Tom Ford bashes people over the head with Very Sweet and Very Very Vanilla. Herod is a masterclass of virtuoso perfumery in comparison.<br />
<br />
All at once it is smoky and spicy and earthy and slightly sweet and oh so creamy in a swirling dance that is unique modern masculine and a best-thing-I-ever-smelled, so delicious that I can’t stop sniffing at it and discerning the different notes.<br />
<br />
Some say it’s too safe or bland or mainstream but I think it is actually a wonderland of niche-quality smells that are used with restraint and perfectly balanced into a complex gentle harmonious masterpiece.<br />
<br />
One thing I haven’t seen many discuss: I believe the key element is the incense, the central nag Champa note that is smoky and woody and slightly sweet/floral and earthy and dark and mysterious that ties all the other notes together. A brilliant bridge between The Smoky tobacco, The spicy sweet cinnamon and pepper, the creamy rich vanilla, the earthy vetiver and musks,  aromatic woods etc. <br />
<br />
I smelled a lot of nag champa incense in my university days and Herod’s incense smells spot on. Nag champa is Indian incense that has unique notes similar to sandalwood and jasmine and plum. Mix those in with cinnamon, cedar, vetiver, musky florals, etc, and that’s why I feel this is so much more complex than “tobacco plus vanilla” and actually a masterpiece of layered perfume blending.<br />
<br />
Unbelievable. I have immediately ordered a 75ml bottle for 120 bucks.<br />
<br />
Update: My 75ml bottle from eBay is a March 2021 batch and smells exactly the same as my sample, maybe a twinge fruitier up front. That’s from the first spray with no maceration. I’m at 5 hour mark from three sprays and still smell it strongly. Sooo delicious and plenty of performance</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="1500063"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=1500063#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="16939" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

Whilst beloved by many, this fragrance just doesn’t work for me. <br />
<br />
I’ve tried this in Arabian summer and European autumn. In the heat, it smells pungent. In the cold, it’s weak. <br />
<br />
Naxos and Side Effect are leagues ahead for sweet tobacco in my opinion. <br />
<br />
6.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="1580134"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=1580134#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1033787" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I'm on the search for my perfect tobacco scent. Unfortunately, this is not it. I wouldn't classify this as tobacco at all. It's diabetic sweet with main notes of vanilla and cinnamon. The tobacco is there, it has a chai-latte-like spicy presence, but it's way in the background. If that's your bag then by all means, go ahead and indulge. <br />
<br />
NOTE: You may however want to try Aramis' Tobacco Reserve first, as you might find more than a few similarities with Herod, for like a fifth of the price. <br />
<br />
Aramis' Tobacco Reserve is a little more green and tonka bean replaces the cinnamon and vanilla. But do try, I find it to be a more refined scent than Herod, but still too sweet for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="16939"comment_id="1198021"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Herod-16939.html?ccid=1198021#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent895430" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
